---

## Web Audit Wave-WEB-2026-04-24 Search S8 — RBAC + backend route gaps

- [ ] WEB-S8-001. **`GET /api/v1/account/usage` requires `authMiddleware` at mount but has no `asyncHandler` wrapper — a thrown promise (e.g. DB unavailable) crashes the process.** `packages/server/src/routes/account.routes.ts` line 9. Fix: wrap the handler with `asyncHandler(async (req, res) => { … })`.

- [ ] WEB-S8-002. **`GET /api/v1/import/repairdesk/status` and `GET /api/v1/import/history` have no role check — any authenticated user (technician, cashier) can read all import run history, including error logs that may contain sensitive API-response fragments.** `packages/server/src/routes/import.routes.ts` lines 346, 436. Fix: add `if (req.user?.role !== 'admin') throw new AppError(…, 403)` at the top of both handlers, identical to the guard on `/start` (line 230).

- [ ] WEB-S8-003. **`GET /api/v1/import/repairshopr/status` and `GET /api/v1/import/myrepairapp/status` same gap as WEB-S8-002.** `packages/server/src/routes/import.routes.ts` lines 722, 1052. Fix: add admin role gate matching `/repairdesk/status`.

- [ ] WEB-S8-004. **`POST /api/v1/catalog/import/:catalogId` (import catalog item to inventory) has no permission gate — any authenticated user can insert inventory rows.** `packages/server/src/routes/catalog.routes.ts` line 162. The sibling `/sync` (line 230) uses `adminOnly`; this mutating endpoint does not. Fix: add `adminOnly` middleware or `requirePermission('inventory.create')`.

- [ ] WEB-S8-005. **`GET /api/v1/catalog/jobs`, `GET /api/v1/catalog/jobs/:id`, `GET /api/v1/catalog/order-queue`, `GET /api/v1/catalog/order-queue/summary`, `GET /api/v1/catalog/stats`, `GET /api/v1/catalog/template-count` — all read-only catalog management endpoints have no role gate; any staff user can enumerate scrape jobs and parts-order queues.** `packages/server/src/routes/catalog.routes.ts` lines 277, 285, 607, 713, 775, 768. Fix: add `requirePermission('inventory.view')` or `adminOnly` for the management-surface endpoints.

- [ ] WEB-S8-006. **`POST /api/v1/catalog/live-search` — triggers an outbound scrape against a supplier website on behalf of the caller; no role check, no per-user rate limit.** `packages/server/src/routes/catalog.routes.ts` line 587. Any technician with a JWT can cause unlimited scrape traffic. Fix: add `requirePermission('inventory.view')` and a per-user `consumeWindowRate` guard (e.g. 10 req/min).

- [ ] WEB-S8-007. **`POST /api/v1/catalog/order-queue/add` and `PATCH /api/v1/catalog/order-queue/:id` — mutate the parts-order queue with no role check.** `packages/server/src/routes/catalog.routes.ts` lines 650, 727. Fix: add `requirePermission('inventory.edit')`.

- [ ] WEB-S8-008. **`GET /api/v1/tickets/tv-display` (inside `tickets.routes.ts`, served under `authMiddleware`) returns `customer_first_name` and `assigned_tech` full name — the data that `tv.routes.ts` deliberately redacted for the unauthenticated TV endpoint is re-exposed here to any authenticated role.** `packages/server/src/routes/tickets.routes.ts` lines 1632–1664. Fix: either restrict to `requireAdminOrManager` or redact PII to match the public TV board shape.

- [ ] WEB-S8-009. **`GET /api/v1/tickets/feedback-summary` and `GET /api/v1/tickets/:id/feedback` have no role gate — technicians and cashiers can read all customer feedback, including `comment` text which may contain PII.** `packages/server/src/routes/tickets.routes.ts` lines 1670, 3821. Fix: add `requirePermission('tickets.view')`.

- [ ] WEB-S8-010. **`POST /api/v1/tickets/:id/feedback` (unauthenticated feedback submission) is mounted under `authMiddleware` globally but has no internal auth check — staff can submit feedback on any ticket under any customer's identity.** `packages/server/src/routes/tickets.routes.ts` line 3833. The endpoint is intended for portal/kiosk use but lives on the authenticated API. Fix: move to a public route (`/public/api/v1/tickets/:id/feedback`) with a rate limit, or confirm this is staff-only and gate with `requirePermission('tickets.edit')`.

- [ ] WEB-S8-011. **`GET /api/v1/tickets/:id/history` and `GET /api/v1/tickets/:id/repair-time` have no permission gate, so a cashier-role user can read full audit history of any ticket (field-by-field change log including user names, old/new values).** `packages/server/src/routes/tickets.routes.ts` lines 2864, 2891. Fix: add `requirePermission('tickets.view')`.

- [ ] WEB-S8-012. **`GET /api/v1/tickets/:id/appointments` has no permission gate.** `packages/server/src/routes/tickets.routes.ts` line 3917. Fix: add `requirePermission('tickets.view')`.

- [ ] WEB-S8-013. **`GET /api/v1/tickets/saved-filters`, `POST /api/v1/tickets/saved-filters`, `DELETE /api/v1/tickets/saved-filters/:id` — saved filters have no ownership isolation beyond `user_id`. `DELETE /saved-filters/:id` queries `WHERE id = ?` without `AND user_id = req.user.id`, allowing one user to delete another user's filter by guessing the numeric ID (IDOR).** `packages/server/src/routes/tickets.routes.ts` lines 1864, 1884, 1917. Fix: add `AND user_id = ?` to the DELETE (and verify fetch on PUT).

- [ ] WEB-S8-014. **`GET /api/v1/reports/tickets` (ticket volume/tech/revenue report) has no `requireAdminOrManager` call — any authenticated technician can read the full revenue-by-tech breakdown.** `packages/server/src/routes/reports.routes.ts` line 709. All other financial report endpoints call `requireAdminOrManager(req)` at the top; this one does not. Fix: add `requireAdminOrManager(req)` as the first line.

- [ ] WEB-S8-015. **`GET /api/v1/reports/customer-acquisition` — the `requireFeature` gate is present but `requireAdminOrManager` is absent; this report returns customer acquisition sources aggregated by month, which is marketing/PII data that technicians should not see.** `packages/server/src/routes/reports.routes.ts` line 1351. Fix: add `requireAdminOrManager(req)`.

- [ ] WEB-S8-016. **`GET /api/v1/reports/presets`, `POST /api/v1/reports/presets`, `PUT /api/v1/reports/presets/:presetId`, `DELETE /api/v1/reports/presets/:presetId` — no role check beyond `authMiddleware`. Any user can create/read/update/delete report presets. The PUT and DELETE check `user_id = req.user.id` ownership correctly, but GET lists all presets for the current user regardless of role — a cashier saving presets for financial reports they cannot see is a UX inconsistency.** `packages/server/src/routes/reports.routes.ts` lines 1471–1600. P2: no data leak, minor inconsistency. Fix: accept current behavior or add `requireAdminOrManager` to constrain preset creation to report-eligible roles.

- [ ] WEB-S8-017. **`GET /api/v1/employees/` (list) and `GET /api/v1/employees/performance/all` have no role check — any staff member can enumerate all employee usernames, emails, roles, and performance metrics (ticket count, revenue).** `packages/server/src/routes/employees.routes.ts` lines 174, 195. Fix: add `requirePermission('employees.view')` or at minimum `requireAdminOrManager`.

- [ ] WEB-S8-018. **`GET /api/v1/roles/permission-keys` has no auth check beyond the global `authMiddleware` — any authenticated user can retrieve the full list of permission key strings.** `packages/server/src/routes/roles.routes.ts` line 116. Low sensitivity (no values, just names) but unnecessarily exposed. Fix: add `requireAdmin(req)` to match all sibling routes.

- [ ] WEB-S8-019. **`GET /api/v1/roles/users/:userId/role` has no role check — any authenticated user can look up the custom role assignment for any user ID (enumeration of role assignments).** `packages/server/src/routes/roles.routes.ts` line 336. Fix: add `requireAdmin(req)`.

- [ ] WEB-S8-020. **`GET /api/v1/settings/config` returns all `store_config` rows to any authenticated user; only `SENSITIVE_CONFIG_KEYS` are filtered for non-admins. But the key set may evolve — new sensitive keys added to the DB without being added to `SENSITIVE_CONFIG_KEYS` silently leak to all staff.** `packages/server/src/routes/settings.routes.ts` line 337. Fix: invert the model — maintain a `PUBLIC_CONFIG_KEYS` allowlist (e.g. `store_name`, `currency`, `timezone`) and return only those to non-admins instead of filtering a denylist.

- [ ] WEB-S8-021. **`GET /api/v1/settings/preferences` and `PUT /api/v1/settings/preferences` — no `asyncHandler` wrapping; both use plain `async (req, res)` directly. An unhandled rejection crashes the worker process.** `packages/server/src/routes/settings.routes.ts` lines 1946, 1959. Fix: wrap both with `asyncHandler(…)`.

- [ ] WEB-S8-022. **`GET /api/v1/settings/setup-status`, `GET /api/v1/settings/store`, `GET /api/v1/settings/statuses`, `GET /api/v1/settings/tax-classes`, `GET /api/v1/settings/payment-methods`, `GET /api/v1/settings/referral-sources`, `GET /api/v1/settings/customer-groups` — all read-only settings endpoints use plain `async (req, res)` without `asyncHandler`. Thrown DB errors cause unhandled promise rejections that crash Express.** `packages/server/src/routes/settings.routes.ts` lines 270, 517, 563, 688, 799, 816, 833. Fix: wrap all handlers with `asyncHandler`.

- [ ] WEB-S8-023. **`GET /api/v1/settings/module-visibility` uses plain `async (req, res)` without `asyncHandler`.** `packages/server/src/routes/settings.routes.ts` line 2004. Fix: wrap with `asyncHandler`.

- [ ] WEB-S8-024. **`GET /api/v1/sms/templates` — reads all SMS templates with no role check (any authenticated user).** `packages/server/src/routes/sms.routes.ts` line 850. Templates contain canned response text that may reveal internal escalation paths or customer-service scripts. Fix: add `requireManagerOrAdmin(req)` to match the write sibling handlers.

- [ ] WEB-S8-025. **`POST /api/v1/sms/preview-template` — substitutes template variables with caller-supplied `vars` object and returns the rendered message; no input size limit on `vars` keys/values; no role check.** `packages/server/src/routes/sms.routes.ts` line 892. Fix: add role gate and bound `vars` object (max 20 keys, each key/value ≤ 200 chars).

- [ ] WEB-S8-026. **`GET /api/v1/team/shifts` reads all team schedules for any `user_id` supplied in the query without a role check — any authenticated user can see any other user's shift schedule.** `packages/server/src/routes/team.routes.ts` line 83 (no role guard; unlike `shiftsSchedule.routes.ts` which silently clamps to self for non-managers). Fix: add the same self-clamp guard as `shiftsSchedule.routes.ts` (lines 87–96) or add `requireAdminOrManager`.

- [ ] WEB-S8-027. **`GET /api/v1/team/goals` reads team goals for any `user_id` without a role check — any staff member can read another employee's performance goals and revenue targets.** `packages/server/src/routes/team.routes.ts` line 480. Fix: if `user_id` is for a different user, require `requireAdminOrManager`.

- [ ] WEB-S8-028. **`GET /api/v1/catalog/order-queue` leaks `customer` first+last name and `order_id` of the associated ticket via the `tickets_json` JOIN — any technician with auth can enumerate which customers have parts on order.** `packages/server/src/routes/catalog.routes.ts` lines 607–649. Fix: restrict with `requirePermission('inventory.view')` (already flagged in WEB-S8-005; noting the PII dimension separately).

- [ ] WEB-S8-029. **`POST /api/v1/import/myrepairapp/nuclear` validates password re-entry but the `confirm` field check (`confirm !== 'NUCLEAR'`) runs BEFORE the role check — a non-admin can probe whether the endpoint exists by omitting `confirm` and getting a 400 (not 403). Minor information leak.** `packages/server/src/routes/import.routes.ts` lines 1135–1154. Fix: move the role check to line 1 of the handler, before any other validation.

- [ ] WEB-S8-030. **`GET /api/v1/import/oauth/status` — reads the current RD OAuth token status without a role check; any authenticated user can confirm whether an OAuth token is active and read its expiry time.** `packages/server/src/routes/import.routes.ts` line 1588. Fix: add `requireAdmin(req)`.

- [ ] WEB-S8-031. **`GET /api/v1/gift-cards/` (list) — no permission gate beyond `authMiddleware`; any staff user can list all gift cards including recipient names and current balances.** `packages/server/src/routes/giftCards.routes.ts` line 104. Fix: add `requirePermission('gift_cards.issue')` or a new `gift_cards.view` permission.

- [ ] WEB-S8-032. **`GET /api/v1/gift-cards/:id` — same issue; no permission gate returns full gift card detail to any authenticated user.** `packages/server/src/routes/giftCards.routes.ts` line 486. Fix: add permission gate matching list.

- [ ] WEB-S8-033. **`GET /api/v1/catalog/parts-search` has no role check — any authenticated user can search the internal parts catalog (supplier prices, SKUs, cost data).** `packages/server/src/routes/catalog.routes.ts` line 568. Fix: add `requirePermission('inventory.view')`.

- [ ] WEB-S8-034. **`GET /api/v1/inventory/manufacturers`, `GET /api/v1/inventory/low-stock`, `GET /api/v1/inventory/summary`, `GET /api/v1/inventory/categories`, `GET /api/v1/inventory/stock-alerts-summary`, `GET /api/v1/inventory/variance-report`, `GET /api/v1/inventory/suppliers/list`, `GET /api/v1/inventory/purchase-orders/list`, `GET /api/v1/inventory/purchase-orders/:id`, `GET /api/v1/inventory/kits`, `GET /api/v1/inventory/kits/:id`, `GET /api/v1/inventory/barcode/:code` — all return without a `requirePermission` gate; these endpoints leak cost prices, supplier names, reorder thresholds and purchase-order details to any authenticated role.** `packages/server/src/routes/inventory.routes.ts` lines 134, 285, 298, 314, 421, 461, 552, 687, 754, 1271, 1339, 1436, 843. Fix: add `requirePermission('inventory.view')` to all read-only inventory endpoints.

- [ ] WEB-S8-035. **`GET /api/v1/inventory/` (main list) wraps with `asyncHandler` but omits `requirePermission` — the top-level list route (the most traffic-heavy endpoint in inventory) has no RBAC gate.** `packages/server/src/routes/inventory.routes.ts` line 64. Fix: add `requirePermission('inventory.view')` as middleware arg before `asyncHandler`.

- [ ] WEB-S8-036. **Rate limiting missing on `POST /api/v1/catalog/live-search` — each call triggers an outbound HTTP scrape against a supplier site. No per-user, no per-tenant, no global cap.** `packages/server/src/routes/catalog.routes.ts` line 587. A single compromised JWT can generate unbounded scrape traffic. Fix: add `consumeWindowRate(req.db, 'catalog_live_search', String(req.user!.id), 10, 60_000)`.

- [ ] WEB-S8-037. **`POST /api/v1/catalog/sync` (trigger supplier catalog scrape) has `adminOnly` guard but no rate limit — an admin session can fire unlimited scrape jobs back-to-back (there is a per-source in-progress lock, but a rapid retry loop floods the `scrape_jobs` table with failed rows).** `packages/server/src/routes/catalog.routes.ts` line 230. Fix: add `consumeWindowRate(req.db, 'catalog_sync', String(req.user!.id), 3, 3_600_000)` (3 per hour).

- [ ] WEB-S8-038. **`GET /api/v1/settings/audit-logs` uses plain `async (req, res)` without `asyncHandler` — all other `adminOnly` handlers in settings use plain async too.** `packages/server/src/routes/settings.routes.ts` line 1807. Covered by a broader pattern; the audit-log endpoint is especially important. Fix: wrap with `asyncHandler`.

- [ ] WEB-S8-039. **Multi-tenant: `GET /api/v1/import/repairdesk/status` (and RS/MRA equivalents) include checkpoint data keyed by `tenantSlug` but use `req.asyncDb` (already tenant-scoped). If the slug resolution fails silently and falls back to `'default'`, checkpoint data from another tenant leaks.** `packages/server/src/routes/import.routes.ts` line 384: `const tenantSlug = (req as any).tenantSlug || 'default'`. Fix: reject with 500 if `req.tenantSlug` is undefined in multi-tenant mode rather than falling back to a shared key.

- [ ] WEB-S8-040. **`GET /api/v1/employees/performance/all` returns `total_revenue` (sum of ticket totals per tech) to any authenticated user — this is financial data.** `packages/server/src/routes/employees.routes.ts` line 195. Fix: add `requireAdminOrManager` gate.

- [ ] WEB-S8-041. **`settings.routes.ts` wide pattern: at least 15 read-only endpoints (statuses, tax-classes, payment-methods, referral-sources, customer-groups, notification-templates, checklist-templates, condition-templates, condition-checks, receipt-templates, webhook-events-enum, sms-providers) use raw `async (req, res)` without `asyncHandler`. An unhandled rejection from any DB call crashes the request thread without an error response.** `packages/server/src/routes/settings.routes.ts` (multiple lines throughout the file). Fix: global search for `async (req, res)` in settings.routes.ts and wrap all with `asyncHandler`.

- [ ] WEB-S8-042. **`POST /api/v1/sms/send` records a rate-limit failure on every successful send (`recordWindowFailure` is called unconditionally after the rate check passes) — this means after 5 sends in 60 s, the 6th send is blocked even if the window counter was correct before the extra increment.** `packages/server/src/routes/sms.routes.ts` line 499: `recordWindowFailure(req.db, 'sms_send', rateLimitKey, 60000)` called on non-failure path. Fix: rename/replace with `recordWindowAttempt` (which doesn't penalize the counter double), or use the atomic `consumeWindowRate` helper.

- [ ] WEB-S8-043. **`GET /api/v1/team/shifts` in `team.routes.ts` (line 83) queries all shifts for all users when no `user_id` filter is given — a manager-or-admin check is absent for the "list all" path, exposing every employee's full shift schedule to any authenticated user.** `packages/server/src/routes/team.routes.ts` lines 83–113. Fix: require `requireAdminOrManager` when `user_id` is absent (all-users query) and clamp to self for non-privileged callers.

- [ ] WEB-S8-044. **`GET /api/v1/inventory/` returns `cost_price` in every inventory row to any authenticated user — cost price is margin-sensitive data that cashiers/technicians should not see.** `packages/server/src/routes/inventory.routes.ts` line 64. Fix: either add `requirePermission('inventory.view')` (which admin/manager roles hold) or project the response to omit `cost_price` for non-privileged roles.

- [ ] WEB-S8-045. **`settings.routes.ts` `GET /settings/users` is gated with `adminOnly` but the returned row shape includes `role` and `is_active` for all users — acceptable. However `PUT /settings/users/:id` (line 962) validates the new `role` against `VALID_ROLES` allowlist but also accepts `permissions` as a raw JSON blob from `req.body`, allowing any admin to write arbitrary permission overrides without schema validation or audit logging.** `packages/server/src/routes/settings.routes.ts` line 962+. Fix: parse and validate `permissions` against `VALID_PERMISSIONS` allowlist keys before storing; write an audit row for every permission change identical to the role-change audit.

---

### Severity summary (Wave S8, 45 findings)

P0 (critical — privilege escalation / unauthenticated mutation / process crash): 5 findings (WEB-S8-001, WEB-S8-004, WEB-S8-006, WEB-S8-010, WEB-S8-042)
P1 (missing role gate on sensitive data / IDOR / missing rate limit on expensive operations): 27 findings (WEB-S8-002 through WEB-S8-009, WEB-S8-011 through WEB-S8-017, WEB-S8-019 through WEB-S8-022, WEB-S8-024 through WEB-S8-031, WEB-S8-034 through WEB-S8-040, WEB-S8-043 through WEB-S8-044)
P2 (information disclosure / minor inconsistency / defense-in-depth): 13 findings (WEB-S8-018, WEB-S8-023, WEB-S8-028, WEB-S8-029, WEB-S8-032 through WEB-S8-033, WEB-S8-041, WEB-S8-045)

Key patterns: (1) Systemic absence of `requirePermission` on read-only inventory, catalog, and employee endpoints — cost prices, supplier data, and employee revenue visible to any role. (2) `import.routes.ts` status/history endpoints lack admin gate matching their sibling start/cancel endpoints. (3) `settings.routes.ts` uses raw `async (req, res)` throughout — ~15 handlers missing `asyncHandler`, creating unhandled-rejection crash vectors. (4) `catalog.routes.ts` import and live-search endpoints are ungated mutations that any authenticated user can call. (5) Tenant-isolation fallback to `'default'` slug in import checkpoints risks cross-tenant data exposure in multi-tenant mode.
### Wave-Loop Finder-I run 2026-04-24 — api/routing/hooks/stores deeper-pass

- [x] WEB-FI-001. **[HIGH] axios `client` has no request `timeout` — long-tail backend stalls hang fetches forever, leaking spinners + react-query promises across tab lifetime.** `api/client.ts:42-46` only sets `baseURL` + `withCredentials`; the public signup client correctly sets `timeout: 15_000` (endpoints.ts:1207) but the authenticated client doesn't. A slow upstream (DB lock, blocked event loop) keeps the request pending; React Query never errors out, error boundaries never trigger, the user sees a forever-spinner. Add `timeout: 30_000` (or per-route override) so failures surface as ECONNABORTED within a bounded window. FIXED 2026-04-24 by Fixer-H — added `DEFAULT_REQUEST_TIMEOUT_MS = 30_000` constant to `packages/web/src/api/client.ts` and wired it into `axios.create` for the authenticated client; per-route callers can still override via `client.post(url, body, { timeout: 60_000 })` for uploads/exports.
  <!-- meta: scope=web/api; files=packages/web/src/api/client.ts:42-46; fix=add-default-timeout+per-route-override -->

- [x] WEB-FI-002. **[HIGH] `superAdminClient` lacks `withCredentials` AND has no timeout — super-admin session bearer is the only auth surface, and every call can stall indefinitely.** `client.ts:301-304`: bare `axios.create({ baseURL: '/super-admin/api', headers: ... })`. No `withCredentials`, no `timeout`. A super-admin tenant impersonation that hangs leaves the operator stuck staring at the spinner; the bearer is the only credential so the SA console has no graceful degradation. Add `timeout: 30_000` and decide explicitly whether SA also wants cookies. FIXED-by-Fixer-ZZ 2026-04-25 — added `timeout: 30_000` to `superAdminClient` `axios.create` matching the tenant client. `withCredentials` left off (SA bearer is the only credential — explicit decision noted in the inline comment).
  <!-- meta: scope=web/api; files=packages/web/src/api/client.ts:301-335; fix=add-timeout+document-withCredentials-policy -->

- [x] WEB-FI-003. **[HIGH] `client.ts` 401-handler retries the original request once via `_retry` but if the retried request still 401s the response is rejected to the caller WITHOUT a logout — the auth store still thinks the user is authenticated.** `client.ts:261-271`. If the new access token is rejected by the server (clock skew, token-version bump, role change between issuance and use), the second 401 falls through to the caller and the user keeps seeing 401 toasts on every action. Add a fallback: if the retried request still 401s, call `forceLogout('session-expired')`. FIXED 2026-04-24 by Fixer-H — wrapped the post-refresh `client(originalRequest)` retry in its own try/catch in `packages/web/src/api/client.ts`; on a second 401 the handler now calls `forceLogout('session-expired')` and rejects the caller. The retry-error status is read via a typed-narrow access (no `any` cast).
  <!-- meta: scope=web/api; files=packages/web/src/api/client.ts:261-271; fix=on-second-401-call-forceLogout-and-suppress-toast -->

- [x] WEB-FI-004. **[HIGH] `client.ts` 5xx auto-toast (line 278-284) fires for EVERY failed mutation including ones with their own `onError` UI — dual toasts on each server error.** Components using `useMutation({ onError: (err) => toast.error(formatApiError(err)) })` already display a toast; the response interceptor unconditionally fires `toast.error('Server error...')` first. User sees two toasts stacked, or worse, a generic "Server error" that overrides a specific server message. Add an opt-out (e.g. `config.skipGlobal500Toast`) or convert to event-bus + opt-in instead. FIXED-by-Fixer-ZZ 2026-04-25 — interceptor now reads `originalRequest.skipGlobal500Toast === true` and short-circuits the global `toast.error` for that request. Default behavior preserved (existing callers unchanged); opting in is `client.post(url, body, { skipGlobal500Toast: true })`.
  <!-- meta: scope=web/api; files=packages/web/src/api/client.ts:278-284; fix=add-opt-out-flag-or-emit-event-instead-of-toast -->

- [ ] WEB-FI-005. **[HIGH] `LOGOUT_REQUIRED_EVENT` listener in `authStore.ts:143` does `window.location.href = '/login'` which throws away the React tree, in-flight uploads, unsaved drafts.** Hard nav defeats `useDraft` (debounced `setTimeout` saves discarded mid-write — losing up to 2s of typed text), pending photo uploads, in-flight WS messages. SPA-internal `Navigate` would preserve drafts and let `auth-cleared` fire to clean up state cleanly. Switch to `react-router` navigation guarded by a "discard or save" prompt for dirty forms.
  <!-- meta: scope=web/stores; files=packages/web/src/stores/authStore.ts:143-156; fix=use-router-navigate-not-window.location.href -->

- [ ] WEB-FI-006. **[MED] `axios.post` for refresh in `performRefresh` calls the BARE `axios` (not the configured `client`), so it never picks up the client default timeout — and crucially has NO timeout of its own.** `client.ts:65-69`: `axios.post(AUTH_REFRESH_URL, {}, { withCredentials, headers })`. A refresh that hangs forever (DNS, slow auth service, network dropout) prevents the 401 retry from EVER resolving — every queued request waits on `sharedRefreshPromise` which never settles. Add an explicit `timeout: 10_000` and reject the slot on timeout so callers fail fast.
  <!-- meta: scope=web/api; files=packages/web/src/api/client.ts:58-80; fix=add-explicit-timeout-on-refresh-axios.post -->

- [x] WEB-FI-007. **[MED] `App.tsx` `ProtectedRoute` does not preserve the user's intended path on redirect — `Navigate to="/login"` drops `from`, so post-login users always land on `/` instead of the deep link they tried to open.** Lines 141. Standard React Router pattern is `<Navigate to="/login" state={{ from: location }} replace />` and the LoginPage reads `location.state?.from?.pathname` after success. Without it, every email-link / bookmarked deep link bounces to dashboard after re-login. (Note: passing `from` via state — NOT a query string — also avoids the `?from=` XSS angle the audit guidelines warn about.) — Fixer-FFF 2026-04-25: ProtectedRoute now passes `state={{ from: location }}`; LoginPage derives a guarded `fromPath` (rejects non-`/`-prefixed and `//`-prefixed values to block off-origin redirect) and uses it in all three post-auth `navigate()` calls (already-auth check, auto-login via `/me`, 2FA verify).
  <!-- meta: scope=web/routing; files=packages/web/src/App.tsx:141; fix=Navigate-with-state.from+LoginPage-redirect-after-login -->

- [ ] WEB-FI-008. **[MED] `App.tsx` `SuperAdminRoute` reads `localStorage.getItem(SUPER_ADMIN_TOKEN_KEY)` once at component-render time but never re-checks — if the token is removed by the response interceptor (401/403), the rendered page stays mounted until the next route navigation.** Lines 184. The component only re-renders when its parent does; revoking SA via the interceptor's `removeItem` doesn't trigger a re-mount. Either subscribe to `SUPER_ADMIN_LOGOUT_EVENT` and force a re-render, or subscribe to the storage event so other tabs also propagate the logout.
  <!-- meta: scope=web/routing; files=packages/web/src/App.tsx:183-198; fix=subscribe-SUPER_ADMIN_LOGOUT_EVENT-or-storage-listener -->

- [ ] WEB-FI-009. **[MED] `main.tsx` global `unhandledrejection` + `error` listeners trigger a hard `window.location.reload()` on any chunk-load error pattern — but the regex is over-broad, matching any user-thrown error containing phrases like "module script".** Lines 122-126,158-170. A user-defined error message with that substring would trigger an infinite-reload loop limited only by the 30-second sentinel. Tighten the predicate to also require `name === 'TypeError'` since real chunk-load failures always surface as TypeError.
  <!-- meta: scope=web/root; files=packages/web/src/main.tsx:122-170; fix=narrow-predicate-to-TypeError+regex-only -->

- [ ] WEB-FI-010. **[MED] `useWebSocket` invalidation map calls `queryClient.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: qk.filter((k) => k !== undefined) })` — `undefined` slots are pruned, but that means a key like `['ticket', undefined]` becomes `['ticket']`, which under tanstack v5 invalidates EVERY query starting with `['ticket']`.** `useWebSocket.ts:277`. Intent is "if id is unknown skip the partial key", actual effect is "match all". When the server sends a `ticket:status_changed` event with a missing id, this re-fetches the ENTIRE ticket subtree across every page. Drop the entry entirely if any required slot is undefined.
  <!-- meta: scope=web/hooks; files=packages/web/src/hooks/useWebSocket.ts:273-296; fix=skip-invalidation-if-required-slot-missing -->

- [ ] WEB-FI-011. **[MED] `useWebSocket` reads the access token in `connect()` and sends it in the `onopen` `auth` message — a token rotated by `performRefresh` between `connect()` and `onopen` firing is captured stale, server rejects with 4001.** `useWebSocket.ts:226,246-249`. Common during 401 burst recovery. Re-read `localStorage.getItem('accessToken')` inside `ws.onopen` immediately before sending so the freshest token wins.
  <!-- meta: scope=web/hooks; files=packages/web/src/hooks/useWebSocket.ts:246-249; fix=re-read-localStorage-inside-ws.onopen -->

- [ ] WEB-FI-012. **[MED] `usePosKeyboardShortcuts` swallows F-keys with `event.preventDefault()` — handlers are read via `handlersRef.current` but if a parent's handler closure captured stale state and is updated only on commit, the F-key fires the previous-render value.** `usePosKeyboardShortcuts.ts:46-74`. Documenting handlers as "must read fresh state via refs/store" is a footgun. Either pass fresh args via a callback registry or document this prominently in the hook header.
  <!-- meta: scope=web/hooks; files=packages/web/src/hooks/usePosKeyboardShortcuts.ts:46-74; fix=document-stale-closure-risk+example-using-store -->

- [x] WEB-FI-013. **[MED] `useDraft` writes to `localStorage` with no per-tenant prefix — drafts written under tenant A are visible to tenant B if the same browser logs into a second tenant on the same origin.** `useDraft.ts:36-48`: keys are caller-supplied (e.g. `'ticket-1234-notes'`) with no tenant scoping. Customer notes / private comments persisted as drafts will leak across tenant logins on the same machine. Either prefix all draft keys with the tenant slug at hook-call sites, or have `useDraft` itself read tenant from `useAuthStore` and prefix automatically. FIXED 2026-04-24 by Fixer-H — `packages/web/src/hooks/useDraft.ts` now resolves every caller-supplied key through `buildScopedKey()` which prefixes `bizarrecrm:draft:<userId>:` (or `bizarrecrm:draft:anon:` when the auth store has not hydrated). Mount, debounced save, and `clearDraft` all use the scoped key; the schedule-time capture (SCAN-601) is preserved via a `scopedKeyRef`.
  <!-- meta: scope=web/hooks; files=packages/web/src/hooks/useDraft.ts:36-94; fix=prefix-key-with-tenant.slug+wipe-on-auth-cleared -->

- [x] WEB-FI-014. **[MED] `useDraft` does not subscribe to `bizarre-crm:auth-cleared` — drafts persist in `localStorage` across logout, exposing the previous user's text on the next sign-in.** Same file as FI-013. The `auth-cleared` listeners in main.tsx + planStore wipe React Query + plan state but `localStorage` draft keys survive. A shared kiosk where Alice writes a sensitive customer note, logs out, Bob logs in — Bob's first visit to the same form restores Alice's draft. Add an `auth-cleared` listener that wipes all keys matching a known draft prefix. FIXED 2026-04-24 by Fixer-H — module-level `addEventListener('bizarre-crm:auth-cleared', wipeAllDrafts)` in `packages/web/src/hooks/useDraft.ts` walks `localStorage` and removes every key matching `^bizarrecrm:draft:`. Runs once on module load, behaves consistently for both mounted and unmounted draft instances, and survives logout / forced-logout / switch-user since all three flows emit `auth-cleared`.
  <!-- meta: scope=web/hooks; files=packages/web/src/hooks/useDraft.ts:1-94; fix=auth-cleared-listener-purges-draft-keys -->

- [ ] WEB-FI-015. **[MED] `confirmStore` resolver-leak guard cancels the previous promise with `false` but leaves the modal-host briefly rendering stale title/message/danger fields.** `confirmStore.ts:25-46`. State is set with `set({ open: true, … })`, but if the host component reads `open` + message via separate selectors, between the prev resolver's `false` resolve and the next render frame the modal can flash old text. Better: include a generation key in state so the modal forcibly remounts on each new confirm() call.

- [ ] WEB-FI-016. **[MED] `authStore.checkAuth` on missing-token path POSTs `/auth/refresh` BEFORE knowing whether a session exists — every fresh tenant subdomain visit fires a refresh attempt that 401s and pollutes server logs.** `authStore.ts:97-130` + `App.tsx:300-338`. On a multi-tenant landing visit, no refresh is needed. Skip the refresh when no `csrf_token` cookie is present (proxy for "we have a session"), or have the server's setup-status response indicate whether a refresh-cookie exists.

- [ ] WEB-FI-017. **[MED] `planStore.fetchPlan` does not abort the in-flight axios request when `auth-cleared` fires — the prior tenant's `/account/usage` can resolve AFTER the listener and `set({ … features: data.features })` writes the OLD tenant's plan into the NEW session.** `planStore.ts:75-143`. - [ ] WEB-FI-018. **[MED] `uiStore` `setTheme` writes localStorage and then `set({ theme })` — between the two, the matchMedia listener (which reads `useUiStore.getState().theme`) can fire and apply the OLD theme one extra time.** `uiStore.ts:72-76,99-102`. Race window is microseconds but the visible mismatch is real on some machines. Reorder: `set({ theme })` first, then `applyTheme`, then `safeWrite`.

- [ ] WEB-FI-019. **[LOW] `client.ts` `forceLogout` calls `logoutClient.post('/auth/logout', …)` with `withCredentials: true` — if logout fires after a user-switch race, the POST may carry the prior user's cookie alongside a new bearer header.** `client.ts:153,166-180`. ### Wave-Loop Finder-G run 2026-04-24 — auth/dashboard/settings deeper-pass

- [ ] WEB-FG-001. **[HIGH] Super-admin JWT stored in `localStorage` is XSS-exfiltratable; one stored-XSS anywhere on the surface yields full cross-tenant impersonation.** `TenantsListPage.tsx:67,251,312` write/read `SUPER_ADMIN_TOKEN_KEY` with `localStorage.setItem/getItem/removeItem`. Token bears the `impersonate(slug)` privilege — a single XSS payload can iterate every tenant + provision a logged-in session for each. Also no `expiresAt` check on read; an expired but un-purged token still flips `isAuthenticated=true` for one render.
  <!-- meta: scope=web/super-admin/auth; files=packages/web/src/pages/super-admin/TenantsListPage.tsx:67,251,312,packages/web/src/api/client.ts; fix=move-super-admin-session-to-httponly-cookie+sliding-refresh+remove-localStorage-fallback -->

- [ ] WEB-FG-002. **[HIGH] `LoginModal` on the public landing page builds a tenant URL purely from user-typed input + `hostname.split('.').slice(-2).join('.')` and `window.location.href=` redirects with no allow-list check.** `LandingPage.tsx:91-97` strips `[^a-z0-9-]` but the registrable-domain heuristic blindly trusts `window.location.hostname` — a customer reaching the landing page through any subdomain of an attacker-controlled DNS entry (e.g. `bizarrecrm.evil-co.com`) gets redirected to `slug.evil-co.com/login`, where a phishing form can harvest credentials. Same heuristic in `SignupPage.tsx:31-36`.
  <!-- meta: scope=web/landing+signup/security; files=packages/web/src/pages/landing/LandingPage.tsx:79-97,packages/web/src/pages/signup/SignupPage.tsx:31-36; fix=hard-code-registrable-domain-from-VITE_PUBLIC_BASE_DOMAIN+reject-redirects-to-other-suffixes -->

- [ ] WEB-FG-003. **[HIGH] Super-admin impersonation has no confirmation dialog and no audit-justification field — single click silently logs operator in as tenant admin.** `TenantsListPage.tsx:231-243` fires `impersonateMutation.mutate()` directly on click; no "type the slug to confirm" step, no required reason string ("ticket #1234 customer support"), and the audit log on the server can't capture intent. Compare to `DangerZoneTab` which gets three-step confirmation for self-service termination yet impersonation (cross-tenant data access) is one click.

- [x] WEB-FG-004. **[HIGH] `EmployeeListPage` PIN modal explicitly states "No PIN set for this employee. Any value will be accepted." — staff with no PIN have no clock-in/out auth at all.** `EmployeeListPage.tsx:147-150` surfaces this client-side, but it means a walk-up bystander on an unattended kiosk can clock in/out any pin-less employee, falsifying timesheets + commissions. Defaults must be "PIN required to clock"; the kiosk path needs a hard-block when `has_pin=0`. FIXED 2026-04-24 by Fixer-H — `packages/web/src/pages/employees/EmployeeListPage.tsx` PinModal now branches on `!employee.has_pin`: instead of an input + "Any value accepted" hint, it renders an amber notice "PIN required to clock in/out — set a 4–6 digit PIN before recording time" and disables the submit button (`disabled={!employee.has_pin || pin.length < 4 || isPending}`). The cancel button label flips to "Close" so the operator can dismiss without a misleading "Cancel" label. Server enforcement is the source of truth; this client gate removes the trivial walk-up attack on unattended kiosks.

- [x] WEB-FG-005. **[HIGH] `BlockChypSettings` posts the entire 16-key form payload (incl. No `dirty` flag (cf. `PosSettings.tsx:51`, `InvoiceSettings.tsx:211`). ### Wave-Loop Finder-H run 2026-04-24 — pos/catalog/inventory deeper-pass

- [x] WEB-FH-001. **[HIGH] POS checkout has NO idempotency key — double-click "Complete Checkout" can charge twice.** `posApi.checkoutWithTicket` (`packages/web/src/api/endpoints.ts:600`) is a bare `api.post('/pos/checkout-with-ticket', data)` with no `X-Idempotency-Key` header, while sibling `invoiceApi.create` + `recordPayment` (lines 249-265) DO send one. The "Complete Checkout" button in `CheckoutModal.tsx:656-663` is only client-side debounced via `processing` state — a slow 5-10s server response with a flaky network re-try (browser auto-retry, user backgrounding+foregrounding the tab, or a quick second click before `setProcessing(true)` paints) creates two invoices + double-charges the customer's card. POS endpoint is the single highest-stakes mutation in the app. FIXED 2026-04-24 by Fixer-G — `posApi.checkoutWithTicket` now sends `X-Idempotency-Key`; key is minted ONCE per cart-session in the unified-pos store (`ensureIdempotencyKey`), persisted across page-refresh, reused by both CheckoutModal + BottomActions create-ticket path, dropped on `clearCart` / `resetAll`.
  <!-- meta: scope=web/api+web/pages/unified-pos; files=packages/web/src/api/endpoints.ts:600,packages/web/src/pages/unified-pos/CheckoutModal.tsx:318-382; fix=add-X-Idempotency-Key-header-on-checkoutWithTicket+per-modal-uuid-stable-across-retries -->

- [x] WEB-FH-002. **[HIGH] Existing idempotency-key generator runs INSIDE the api function — every call (including retries) mints a fresh UUID, defeating the cache.** Pattern at `endpoints.ts:252-254` calls `globalThis.crypto?.randomUUID()` inside the `create` function body. If the user double-clicks, the second call generates a different key and the server sees two distinct requests. The idempotent middleware caches by `(user,url,key)` so the second call is processed as new. Same gap on `recordPayment` line 263. The "DA-6" comment claim is incorrect — keys must be stable across retries (form-scoped, not call-scoped). FIXED 2026-04-24 by Fixer-G — `invoiceApi.create`, `invoiceApi.recordPayment`, and `posApi.checkoutWithTicket` now accept an optional `idempotencyKey` argument that callers mint ONCE at form-open / cart-create and pass on every retry; internal mint kept only as a fallback for legacy callers until they migrate.
  <!-- meta: scope=web/api; files=packages/web/src/api/endpoints.ts:246-265; fix=accept-key-as-arg-and-mint-once-per-form-submit-then-pass-on-retries -->

- [x] WEB-FH-003. **[HIGH] LeftPanel Enter+Click race fires `addProduct` twice for the same item.** `UnifiedSearchBar` has both `onKeyDown(e.key==='Enter') -> results[0].action()` (line 196-200) AND each result's `onMouseDown(e.preventDefault(); r.action())` (line 211). Pressing Enter while clicking the first result OR scanning a barcode that emits Enter+chars fires `addProduct` twice — cart shows qty=2. Same hazard in `BarcodeSearch.handleKey` (line 343-370): no in-flight guard, so two rapid scanner emissions both call `posApi.products` + `addProduct`. Compounds the no-idempotency issue. FIXED 2026-04-24 by Fixer-G — added `actionInFlightRef` + `fireOnce()` wrapper in `UnifiedSearchBar` (250 ms cooldown applied symmetrically on Enter-keydown + onMouseDown), and `scanInFlightRef` lock in `BarcodeSearch.handleKey` released in `finally` block so failed scans don't deadlock the input.
  <!-- meta: scope=web/pages/unified-pos; files=packages/web/src/pages/unified-pos/LeftPanel.tsx:196-200,211,343-370; fix=in-flight-ref-set-true-on-Enter+release-on-action-complete+ignore-duplicate-events-within-150ms -->

- [x] WEB-FH-004. **[HIGH] Product cart has zero stock-cap — clicking a product 5x when only 2 in stock builds a cart of 5, server rejects at checkout.** `ProductsTab.tsx:43-56` only blocks when `in_stock === 0` (button `disabled`), but `addProduct` increments quantity unconditionally (`store.ts:127-141`). Same in `LeftPanel.UnifiedSearchBar` add-product action (line 132-140) and `BarcodeSearch.handleKey` (line 352-362). User builds full cart, walks to terminal, server rejects with stock conflict — bad UX + locks the cart. Should clamp `quantity = Math.min(currentQty+1, in_stock)` and toast on cap. FIXED 2026-04-24 by Fixer-G — `store.addProduct` now accepts `{ stockCap }` opts and clamps qty via `Math.min(currentQty+1, stockCap)`; ProductsTab + LeftPanel UnifiedSearchBar add-action + BarcodeSearch all pass `product.in_stock` (services skip the cap), pre-check the cap before calling and toast `"Only N of … in stock"` when the cashier hits the ceiling.
  <!-- meta: scope=web/pages/unified-pos; files=packages/web/src/pages/unified-pos/store.ts:126-141,packages/web/src/pages/unified-pos/ProductsTab.tsx:43-56,packages/web/src/pages/unified-pos/LeftPanel.tsx:132-140,352-362; fix=cap-quantity-at-product.in_stock+toast-when-cap-reached+gray-add-button -->

- [x] WEB-FH-005. FIXED 2026-04-24 by Fixer-O — extracted shared cents-int totals helper at `packages/web/src/pages/unified-pos/totals.ts`; `LeftPanel.useTotals` and `CheckoutModal.useCheckoutTotals` now both delegate to `computePosTotals(...)`, which converts each line to integer cents up front, applies the WEB-FH-006 pro-rata discount allocation on integers, and divides by 100 only once at display. Eliminates the 1¢ drift between cart panel, checkout modal, and the server's cents-pure recompute. **[HIGH] POS totals computed in floats with toFixed(2) / Math.round(x*100)/100 chains — not cents-pure.** `LeftPanel.useTotals` lines 706-753 + `CheckoutModal.useCheckoutTotals` lines 29-75 BOTH duplicate the same float-discount-tax-total math. Each step is `Math.round(x * 100) / 100` then re-multiplied — classic 0.1+0.2=0.30000000000000004 rounding drift. A 27-line cart with mixed taxable/non-taxable can drift 1c between LeftPanel display, CheckoutModal display, and the server's cents-pure recompute. Server already migrated POS sale to cents-int (POS-SALES-001). Duplicate hand-rolled float math is the visible client gap.
  <!-- meta: scope=web/pages/unified-pos; files=packages/web/src/pages/unified-pos/LeftPanel.tsx:706-753,packages/web/src/pages/unified-pos/CheckoutModal.tsx:29-75; fix=extract-shared-cents-int-totals-helper+round-once-at-display-only -->

- [x] WEB-FH-006. **[HIGH] Tax computed on FULL pre-discount taxable amount even when discount is applied — sales-tax over-charged on every discounted sale.** `LeftPanel.useTotals` line 747: `tax = taxableAmount * taxRate`, then `total = subtotal + tax - discountAmount`. A $100 taxable item with 10% off (`discount=10`) is taxed on $100 -> $8.86 tax, total $98.86. In most US states (CA, TX, NY, FL) sales tax is on the DISCOUNTED price ($90 -> $7.98) — store is over-collecting tax + paying excess to the state. Same drift on member-discount path (line 736-744). No tenant policy toggle for tax-on-discount. FIXED 2026-04-24 by Fixer-G — both `LeftPanel.useTotals` AND `CheckoutModal.useCheckoutTotals` now allocate `discountAmount` pro-rata across taxable lines (`taxableShareOfDiscount = discountAmount * (taxableAmount / subtotal)`), tax on `Math.max(0, taxableAmount - taxableShareOfDiscount)`. Falls back to "tax on full taxable" only when subtotal == 0 (empty cart edge).
  <!-- meta: scope=web/pages/unified-pos; files=packages/web/src/pages/unified-pos/LeftPanel.tsx:706-753,packages/web/src/pages/unified-pos/CheckoutModal.tsx:33-75; fix=allocate-discount-pro-rata-across-taxable-lines+tax-on-net+settings.tax_on_discounted-toggle -->

Tenant configures 7% sales tax -> cart still SAYS "Tax (8.865%)" but tax amount is computed on 7%. Customer sees 7% charge under an 8.865% label and disputes; auditor sees inconsistent record. Drift introduced when default tax rate moved into a hook (useDefaultTaxRate) but the label string was missed. Same bug not present in `CheckoutModal` which omits the rate label entirely. FIXED 2026-04-24 by Fixer-G — replaced literal `"Tax (8.865%)"` with `Tax ({(taxRate * 100).toLocaleString(undefined, { maximumFractionDigits: 3 })}%)` so the label tracks live tenant config (handles 7%, 7.625%, 8.875%, 10% without trailing zeros).

### Wave-Loop Finder-J run 2026-04-24 — secrets/PII/audit-trail/cache

- [x] WEB-FJ-001. **[HIGH] Access token + super-admin token both stored in `localStorage` — any XSS reads them and the SA token grants tenant-impersonation across the whole estate.** FIXED 2026-04-24 by Fixer-L — moved super-admin token to `sessionStorage` via a centralised `superAdminTokenStore` helper (token dies with tab, no cross-tab `storage` leak). Helper auto-migrates any legacy localStorage value on first read. All call-sites (App.tsx route guard, TenantsListPage login + sign-out, client.ts request/response interceptors) now go through the helper. httpOnly-cookie path left for a server-coordinated change. `stores/authStore.ts:67,92,104,122` + `api/client.ts:298,307,323-324` + `pages/super-admin/TenantsListPage.tsx:67`. SUPER_ADMIN_TOKEN_KEY=`'superAdminToken'` sits in plain localStorage; once stolen, the attacker calls `POST /super-admin/api/tenants/{slug}/impersonate` and lands a tenant JWT for any shop. Industry guidance is to keep refresh + super-admin tokens in httpOnly cookies; only the short-lived access token may be in JS-reachable storage and only when CSP is strict. Code already keeps the refresh token cookie-side — close the loop on the SA path.
  <!-- meta: scope=web/api+web/stores+web/pages/super-admin; files=packages/web/src/stores/authStore.ts:67,92,104,122,packages/web/src/api/client.ts:298-340,packages/web/src/pages/super-admin/TenantsListPage.tsx:67; fix=move-superAdminToken-to-httpOnly-cookie+server-issued-Set-Cookie+remove-localStorage-set/get -->

- [ ] WEB-FJ-002. **[HIGH] Customer photo URLs `/uploads/{file_path}` are unsigned + non-expiring — anyone with a URL keeps access forever, even after the customer is "PII-erased".** `pages/tickets/TicketDevices.tsx:942,961,1037,1056,1057` + `pages/customers/components/PhotoMementosWallet.tsx:108`. Hard-coded path means if a customer leaks/forwards a photo URL (cracked-screen evidence, ID scan, accessory photo), or if it ends up in a CDN/proxy log, retrieval is permanent. Worse, the `privacyApi.eraseCustomerPii` flow (endpoints.ts:1240) presumably nulls customer PII rows but leaves the file blobs at the same predictable path. GDPR Art.17 ("right to erasure") needs the photo URL itself to revoke, not just the FK.
  <!-- meta: scope=web/pages/tickets+pages/customers; files=packages/web/src/pages/tickets/TicketDevices.tsx:942-1057,packages/web/src/pages/customers/components/PhotoMementosWallet.tsx:108; fix=server-issue-short-lived-signed-URL-via-/photos/:id/url+rotate-key-on-erase-PII+web-fetches-via-blob+revokeObjectURL -->

- [ ] WEB-FJ-003. **[HIGH] WebSocket auth token sent as plain JSON frame `ws.send({type:'auth', token})` — token sits in browser DevTools "Frames" view + intermediate proxies / corporate-MITM logs.** `hooks/useWebSocket.ts:248`. Industry-standard auth for WS is via the upgrade-handshake `Sec-WebSocket-Protocol` header (which axios-style http-only cookies can also handle via `withCredentials`). Sending the JWT as a normal text frame after open means: (a) the token is visible in any tool that records frames, (b) the same token then sits in `wsRef.current` closure for the lifetime of the tab — long after a refresh has rotated the access token. A 401 reject + reconnect path also re-sends the same potentially-stale JWT, which can trigger upstream rate limit on bad-token attempts.
  <!-- meta: scope=web/hooks; files=packages/web/src/hooks/useWebSocket.ts:248,209,236-249; fix=auth-during-handshake-via-Cookie/Sec-WebSocket-Protocol+server-validates-on-Upgrade+drop-the-{type:auth}-frame -->

- [ ] WEB-FJ-004. **[HIGH] SMS draft compose text persists in `localStorage` keyed by raw phone number — every keystroke a staff member types into a customer chat is mirrored to disk under `draft_sms_+15551234567` until cleared.** `hooks/useDraft.ts:73` + `pages/communications/CommunicationPage.tsx:979`. Drafts hold message bodies (often sensitive: medical-device repairs, addresses, account-recovery codes, "your phone is ready, here's the door code"), are debounced-saved every 2s, and survive logout. Anyone with shared-PC access (counter staff after-hours, IT support, Apple-store-style demo machines) can dump localStorage and harvest phone-number → message-body pairs. Same hazard for `draft_note_ticket_*` with private repair notes.
  <!-- meta: scope=web/hooks+pages/communications+pages/tickets; files=packages/web/src/hooks/useDraft.ts:73,packages/web/src/pages/communications/CommunicationPage.tsx:979,packages/web/src/pages/tickets/TicketNotes.tsx:54; fix=move-drafts-to-sessionStorage-or-IndexedDB-with-encryption+clear-on-logout-via-auth-cleared-event+exclude-phone-from-key-(use-conversation-id) -->

- [x] WEB-FJ-006. **[HIGH] `localStorage['recent_views']` stores customer + ticket NAMES (PII) indefinitely — never cleared on logout, leaks last-seen identities to next user of shared kiosk PC.** `pages/customers/CustomerDetailPage.tsx:120-137` + `pages/tickets/TicketDetailPage.tsx:362` + `components/layout/Sidebar.tsx:259`. Up to 20 recent customer/ticket entries with `label = "${first_name} ${last_name}"` survive `authStore.logout()` (which only removes accessToken). - [x] WEB-FJ-007. **[HIGH] `console.warn('Token refresh failed, logging out:', refreshErr)` runs UNCONDITIONALLY in production — refreshErr serialises the failed request config including any tokens in headers/cookies into the browser console.** `api/client.ts:268,298`. The dev-only path at line 221-231 is correctly gated on `import.meta.env.DEV`, BUT the four `console.warn` calls at lines 30, 111, 121, 124, 173, 245, 251, 268, 298 are not. In production, a third-party browser-error shipper (Sentry, Datadog RUM, LogRocket) capturing console output forwards `refreshErr.config.url` which includes `/auth/refresh` + the request body which includes the CSRF token, plus any pending Authorization header. Industry baseline: production console output must not contain auth payloads or correlation ids that survive into shipper logs.
  FIXED-by-Fixer-JJJ 2026-04-25 — Added a `devWarn` shim in `api/client.ts` that resolves to `console.warn` only when `import.meta.env.DEV` is truthy and is a no-op in production. Replaced every diagnostic `console.warn` callsite in client.ts (emit-logout, proactive-refresh, token-decode, logout endpoint, upgrade-modal lazy load, retry-401, refresh-failed, super-admin-logout). Production bundles no longer ship refreshErr / config / Authorization headers to browser console output, so RUM shippers (Sentry/Datadog/LogRocket) can't capture them.
  <!-- meta: scope=web/api; files=packages/web/src/api/client.ts:30,111,121,124,173,245,251,268,298; fix=guard-all-console.warn-on-import.meta.env.DEV+sanitize-error.config-(strip-Authorization+Cookie+X-CSRF-Token-headers)-before-logging -->

- [ ] WEB-FJ-008. **[MED] Photo-capture page accepts staff-bearer token via `?t=` URL query param — the token leaks via Referer when any IMG loads from another origin AND lives in browser history.** `pages/photo-capture/PhotoCapturePage.tsx:10,72`. A QR-scanned link `https://shop.example.com/photo-capture/123/45?t=eyJhbG...` is shared to the customer's phone for them to upload device photos. The token is then passed as `Authorization: Bearer ${token}`, but it's also in `window.location.search` for the entire session. If the page renders any external IMG (e.g. logo CDN or analytics pixel from `/api/getEmbedConfig`-style branding), Referer carries the full URL including `?t=`. Also persisted in customer's browser history → Chrome Sync → cloud. Should accept the token via `Authorization`-only (e.g. POST a body with token then strip), or `replaceState` it out of the URL on mount like CustomerPortalPage does for its tokenParam.
  <!-- meta: scope=web/pages/photo-capture; files=packages/web/src/pages/photo-capture/PhotoCapturePage.tsx:8-15,71-73; fix=on-mount-history.replaceState-stripping-?t-param+keep-token-only-in-React-state+add-Referrer-Policy:no-referrer-meta-tag -->

- [ ] WEB-FJ-009. **[MED] `customerApi.exportData` GDPR/CCPA export blob is generated client-side as plain JSON Blob — no Content-Disposition `filename*=UTF-8''` encoding + no encryption-at-rest option for the customer.** `pages/customers/CustomerDetailPage.tsx:252-270`. Dumps full `exportPayload` into `Blob([JSON.stringify(...)], 'application/json')` and `a.click()`s into the staff member's Downloads folder where it sits unencrypted. A typical export contains every PII field the system holds plus invoices and ticket notes. Industry GDPR practice is to (a) email a signed link to the customer rather than letting staff download it, (b) optionally pgp/age-encrypt with a customer-supplied passphrase, (c) honour Content-Disposition so accented filenames don't mojibake. None of those are present.
  <!-- meta: scope=web/pages/customers; files=packages/web/src/pages/customers/CustomerDetailPage.tsx:252-270; fix=server-builds-export+emails-signed-time-limited-link-direct-to-customer+staff-only-triggers+remove-client-Blob-path -->

- [ ] WEB-FJ-010. **[MED] Magic-link portal token written to `sessionStorage['portal_token']` after `replaceState` — token survives until tab close, no idle-timeout, no rotation on use.** `pages/portal/CustomerPortalPage.tsx:71` + `pages/portal/usePortalAuth.ts:25,60`. The verify call returns success but the same long-lived token is reused for every subsequent `Authorization: Bearer ${token}` call (portalApi.ts:38). If the customer leaves the portal tab open on a public computer (library, hotel kiosk), anyone touching the keyboard has a still-valid session. Web-portal industry baseline is rotate-on-use OR a 15-minute idle timeout — neither here. `sessionStorage` clears on tab close, but tabs hibernate / restore-on-relaunch in Chrome with iCloud-tab sync, defeating the assumption.
  <!-- meta: scope=web/pages/portal; files=packages/web/src/pages/portal/CustomerPortalPage.tsx:71,packages/web/src/pages/portal/usePortalAuth.ts:25-44,60-69; fix=add-idle-timeout-15min-via-setTimeout-on-user-activity+server-rotates-token-on-each-verifySession+drop-token-on-visibilitychange:hidden-after-N-min -->

- [ ] WEB-FJ-011. **[MED] `customer.exportData` JSON download filename `customer-${id}-data-export-${date}.json` includes only the numeric customer-id but no tenant slug — staff downloading multiple tenants' data via super-admin impersonation gets colliding filenames + cross-tenant data mix-up risk.** `pages/customers/CustomerDetailPage.tsx:261`. Super-admin impersonates Tenant A, exports customer #5 → `customer-5-data-export-2026-04-24.json`. Switches tenants, exports Tenant B's customer #5 the same day → same filename, default browser appends ` (1)`. Staff later opens `customer-5-data-export-2026-04-24.json` thinking it's Tenant A and emails it to the wrong customer. Include tenant_slug in the filename.
  <!-- meta: scope=web/pages/customers; files=packages/web/src/pages/customers/CustomerDetailPage.tsx:255-262; fix=read-impersonation-session-or-current-tenant-slug-and-prefix-filename -->

- [ ] WEB-FJ-012. **[MED] `getImpersonationSession()` reads `localStorage['impersonation_session']` with tenant_slug AND tenant_name — survives logout (only `clearImpersonationSession()` clears it, called only on the explicit "Exit" button).** `components/ImpersonationBanner.tsx:6,22,28`. If the SA closes the browser, reopens, the banner state can re-mount without the SA actually being re-authenticated — the SA token may be gone but the banner still trusts the impersonation marker. Worse: a tenant operator with localStorage access can hand-craft `impersonation_session={tenant_slug:"competitor-shop"}` and the banner shows "Impersonating competitor-shop" misleading the next staff member. Should validate against an active SA session and clear the impersonation marker on the standard `auth-cleared` event.
  <!-- meta: scope=web/components; files=packages/web/src/components/ImpersonationBanner.tsx:6-43,75-79; fix=auth-cleared-listener-also-clears-impersonation_session+banner-only-renders-when-SA-token-is-also-present -->

- [ ] WEB-FJ-013. **[MED] `signupApi.createShop` POSTs admin password as a top-level JSON body field with no client-side hash + no breached-password check — works against `/api/v1/signup`.** `pages/signup/SignupPage.tsx:213-219` + `api/endpoints.ts:1234`. Modern signup flows prefilter against haveibeenpwned k-anonymity API client-side ("this password has been seen in 273k breaches") before submitting. Server-side bcrypt is fine but doesn't help the user who picks `password123`. Combined with the only client validation being `password.length < 8` (line 190), the system actively encourages weak passwords. Industry baseline is HIBP range query + zxcvbn strength meter.
  <!-- meta: scope=web/pages/signup; files=packages/web/src/pages/signup/SignupPage.tsx:190,213-219; fix=add-haveibeenpwned-range-API-check+block-on-Pwned-or-zxcvbn-score-<-3+show-strength-meter -->

- [ ] WEB-FJ-014. **[MED] `customer-pay/${token}/click` analytics-tracking POST runs on EVERY load, including bot crawls + accidental refreshes — no debounce, no client-side rate limit.** `pages/billing/CustomerPayPage.tsx:64-66`. A user reloading the page 5 times to "make sure" each fires a POST; a Slack/iMessage link unfurl previewer (which fetches the page server-side then bot-crawls links) fires it once per preview. Click-conversion analytics are now polluted with non-user activity, and worse, the token is hit publicly on every preview, exposing the existence/status of a payment link to anyone the customer mentions it to. Should fire only after a user action (button click) or once per session via sessionStorage marker.
  <!-- meta: scope=web/pages/billing; files=packages/web/src/pages/billing/CustomerPayPage.tsx:64-66; fix=fire-click-tracking-only-after-user-interaction-or-cap-once-per-token-per-sessionStorage -->

- [ ] WEB-FJ-015. **[MED] No `Cache-Control` / `Pragma` meta tags on auth-protected HTML routes — same-origin browser back-button after logout shows the previous user's authenticated dashboard contents (cached HTML render).** Search across `App.tsx`, `main.tsx`, `index.html` shows zero `<meta http-equiv="Cache-Control">`. SPA routing means the underlying React tree re-renders with new auth state after logout, BUT browser DOM Cache (BFCache) on Safari + Firefox restores the prior render including any in-DOM PII (customer name, phone, last 4 of card) for ~1s before React reconciles. OWASP "Sensitive Data Caching" recommends `Cache-Control: no-store, no-cache, must-revalidate` for authenticated pages. Server may set them but missing meta-tag belt-and-suspenders means iOS WebView / Safari shows a flash of cached PII.
  <!-- meta: scope=web/index.html+main.tsx; files=packages/web/index.html,packages/web/src/main.tsx; fix=add-meta-Cache-Control:no-store-on-document-head+pageshow-listener-evicts-bfcache-via-window.location.reload-when-event.persisted -->

- [ ] WEB-FJ-016. **[MED] CommandPalette stores raw user search queries in sessionStorage `crm_recent_searches` — searches typically contain customer names, phone fragments, ticket numbers.** `components/shared/CommandPalette.tsx:34-86`. TTL is 24h but stored as plain strings; the staff member who searches "John Smith 555" leaves a sessionStorage trail of all the customers they investigated. Even sessionStorage is dumped to disk on tab restore + survives "log out and hand laptop to colleague" within the same tab session. No clear-on-logout listener (the `auth-cleared` event isn't subscribed). Clears only on `removeItem` corruption path.
  <!-- meta: scope=web/components/shared; files=packages/web/src/components/shared/CommandPalette.tsx:34-86; fix=auth-cleared-listener-removes-RECENT_SEARCHES_KEY+optionally-hash-queries-with-stable-pepper-before-storage -->

- [ ] WEB-FJ-017. **[LOW] `wallet-pass` blob URL revoked after 60s but the new tab keeps the document live — once the timer fires, hitting "back" or "reload" in that tab gives a broken page with no error.** `pages/customers/CustomerDetailPage.tsx:202-210`. The 60s cap was chosen for memory hygiene but the wallet-pass HTML is the customer's loyalty pass; the staff member opens it expecting to be able to print or screenshot. After 60s it 404s in the popup with no toast (popup is a different window, the parent's toast doesn't fire). Bump to 5min OR keep alive until popup `unload`.
  <!-- meta: scope=web/pages/customers; files=packages/web/src/pages/customers/CustomerDetailPage.tsx:198-211; fix=listen-to-popup-window-unload-event-and-revoke-then-or-bump-timer-to-5-min -->

- [ ] WEB-FJ-018. **[LOW] Portal auto-login error "verification failed" surfaces only as a toast — token is REMOVED from URL FIRST, so the customer can't share/screenshot the bad link to support.** `pages/portal/CustomerPortalPage.tsx:64-86`. The `replaceState` to strip the token (line 64-66) runs before the `verifySession` resolves. If verification fails, the customer sees a toast on a now-bare URL `/customer-portal` and can't tell what link they clicked. They contact support, support has no token to inspect server-side. Capture the token into React state first, replaceState only AFTER successful verify, and on failure surface "your link XYZ123 expired" with the trailing 6 chars.
  <!-- meta: scope=web/pages/portal; files=packages/web/src/pages/portal/CustomerPortalPage.tsx:62-87; fix=keep-token-tail-in-error-toast+replaceState-only-after-successful-verifySession-or-leave-it-and-server-burns-on-success -->

- [ ] WEB-FJ-019. **[LOW] `signupApi.createShop` errors surface server `apiErr?.response?.data?.message` raw — server validation can include the email being signed up with, exposing it via shoulder-surfing or screenshot.** `pages/signup/SignupPage.tsx:224-230`. If server returns `{ message: "An account already exists for serega@example.com" }`, the email gets rendered into setApiError → visible on the unauthenticated landing page. Industry baseline is "If your email is already registered, we sent a reset link" without echoing the address. Same gap on `LoginPage.tsx` `formatApiError` paths.
  <!-- meta: scope=web/pages/signup+pages/auth; files=packages/web/src/pages/signup/SignupPage.tsx:224-230,packages/web/src/pages/auth/LoginPage.tsx; fix=server-returns-generic-message+web-prefers-message-from-known-allowlist+strip-emails-from-error-bodies-before-render -->

- [ ] WEB-FJ-020. **[LOW] `tel:` and `mailto:` links carry full PII in the URL — when used inside the portal iframe widget mode, Referer/click tracker forwards the full address to any analytics on the embed page.** `components/shared/CustomerPreviewPopover.tsx:111` + `pages/customers/CustomerListPage.tsx:925,936` + `pages/portal/PortalDashboard.tsx:148,156`. Industry doesn't typically worry about `tel:` referer (browsers strip), but the link `<a href="mailto:customer@example.com">` IS clickable by anyone watching a screen-share of the customer-list page, and its text content is the literal email. Combined with the portal widget mode (`?mode=widget` iframe in 3rd-party site), the embedding site's DOM-scraping analytics (Hotjar, FullStory) record the email value. Add `rel="noreferrer noopener"` and consider mask-on-display ("c***@example.com") with click-to-reveal in the portal widget context.
  <!-- meta: scope=web/components/shared+pages/portal; files=packages/web/src/components/shared/CustomerPreviewPopover.tsx:111,packages/web/src/pages/portal/PortalDashboard.tsx:148-156,packages/web/src/pages/customers/CustomerListPage.tsx:925-936; fix=portal-widget-renders-masked-contact+rel=noreferrer-on-mailto+log-mailto-click-to-server-not-clientside -->

- [ ] WEB-FN-005. **[MED] Pagination param drift — server reads `pagesize` (most routes), `per_page` (gift-cards, loaners), and `limit` (catalog/teamChat/super-admin/inventory.low-stock), and within a single endpoint the request key is `pagesize` while the response key is `per_page`.** Examples: `inventoryApi.list` sends `pagesize` to `GET /inventory` (server reads `pagesize` ✓ but RESPONSE pagination key is `per_page` — inventory.routes.ts:127); `voiceApi.calls` sends `pagesize` (server reads `pagesize` ✓, response `per_page` — voice.routes.ts:181,218); `giftCardApi.list` sends `per_page` (server reads `per_page` ✓ — giftCards.routes.ts:122,145); `loanerApi.list` sends `per_page` (server reads `per_page` ✓). The query-vs-response asymmetry within a single endpoint plus the cross-endpoint inconsistency makes a generic `usePaginatedQuery` hook impossible — each caller hand-rolls. Industry baseline: settle on one name in both directions and add a server alias for the legacy.

### Wave-Loop Finder-O run 2026-04-24 — concurrency + real-time + multi-tab

- [x] WEB-FO-001. **[HIGH] No optimistic-concurrency / version check on ticket mutations — last-write-wins silently overwrites a co-worker's edits.** FIXED 2026-04-24 by Fixer-L — global axios response interceptor now surfaces 409 Conflict on PUT/PATCH/POST/DELETE with a deduped toast ("This item was updated elsewhere — refresh to see the latest changes."). Server-side If-Match plumbing left for a larger change. `pages/tickets/TicketDetailPage.tsx:252-294` (changeStatusMut), `pages/tickets/KanbanBoard.tsx:147-182`, `pages/tickets/TicketSidebar.tsx:421` (assignee), `pages/tickets/TicketNotes.tsx:68-99`. PUT/PATCH calls send no `If-Match`, no `version`, no `updated_at`-based guard, no 409 surfacing. Two techs editing the same ticket: B's "in repair" status flip silently overwrites A's "ready for pickup" 200 ms earlier — A only notices when WS invalidation refetches and the status pill jumps under their cursor. Critical for repair-shop workflow where multiple techs touch one ticket. Fix: send `if_match: ticket.updated_at` (or numeric `version`) in mutation body; server returns 409 on mismatch; client surfaces "This ticket was changed by someone else — refresh to see latest" and discards the optimistic write.
  <!-- meta: scope=web/pages/tickets+server/routes/tickets; files=packages/web/src/pages/tickets/TicketDetailPage.tsx:252,packages/web/src/pages/tickets/KanbanBoard.tsx:147,packages/web/src/pages/tickets/TicketSidebar.tsx:421; fix=add-version-or-If-Match-header+server-returns-409+client-shows-conflict-banner-and-discards-optimistic -->

- [x] WEB-FO-002. **[HIGH] Two tabs of the same user — Zustand stores never sync; one tab's logout/theme/sidebar/POS-cart state invisible to the other.** FIXED 2026-04-24 by Fixer-L — authStore now subscribes to window `storage` events at module scope: `accessToken` removal in another tab triggers immediate logout + redirect; token add/change triggers `emitAuthCleared()` + `checkAuth()` so the other tab silently re-hydrates. uiStore/POS-cart left for a follow-up. `stores/authStore.ts`, `stores/uiStore.ts`, `stores/planStore.ts`, `stores/confirmStore.ts`, `pages/unified-pos/store.ts`. None of these stores subscribe to `storage` events. POS cart in tab A persists to localStorage but tab B doesn't react until next page load. Worse: log out in tab A → tab B keeps showing protected pages (auth-cleared CustomEvent doesn't cross tabs) until next API call returns 401. Theme/sidebar collapse changed in tab A → tab B keeps old visual state. Fix: add `window.addEventListener('storage', …)` adaptor at module scope per store that pulls the relevant key on cross-tab change, OR migrate to BroadcastChannel for first-class cross-tab sync.
  <!-- meta: scope=web/stores+web/pages/unified-pos; files=packages/web/src/stores/authStore.ts,packages/web/src/stores/uiStore.ts,packages/web/src/pages/unified-pos/store.ts:258-290; fix=BroadcastChannel-or-storage-event-listener-per-store+rehydrate-on-cross-tab-mutation -->

- [x] WEB-FO-003. **[HIGH] WebSocket has no client heartbeat / ping — NAT idle timeouts (60-300 s on cellular and corp NAT) silently drop the socket without firing onclose, leaving the page "connected" forever with no events.** FIXED 2026-04-24 by Fixer-L — useWebSocket sends `{type:'ping'}` every 30 s once authed, tracks lastMessageAt on every onmessage; if 60 s elapse with no traffic the watchdog force-closes (code 4000) so onclose fires reconnect. `pong` messages are short-circuited before the invalidation map. `hooks/useWebSocket.ts:188-399`. The hook handles backoff + visibility + auth, but never sends a `{type:'ping'}` keepalive and never tracks "last message received" to detect a half-open socket. Browsers do not send TCP keepalives at the WS layer. On a busy front-of-house tablet behind store NAT, the socket appears alive (isConnected=true) but new tickets/SMS quietly stop arriving. Fix: send `ping` every 30 s; expect server pong within 10 s; on miss, force `ws.close()` to trigger reconnect.
  <!-- meta: scope=web/hooks; files=packages/web/src/hooks/useWebSocket.ts:188-399; fix=interval-ping-30s+pong-deadline-watchdog+force-close-on-miss-to-trigger-reconnect-flow -->

- [x] WEB-FO-004. **[HIGH] No offline indicator anywhere — `navigator.onLine` is never read, no `online`/`offline` listeners, no banner.** FIXED 2026-04-24 by Fixer-L — new `OfflineBanner` component listens to window `online`/`offline` events and renders an amber bar above the AppShell content whenever the browser reports offline. Mounted between ImpersonationBanner and Header. Searched all of `packages/web/src/`. Service worker is intentionally unregistered (`public/sw.js`). When the wifi router reboots mid-checkout, the cashier sees spinners and 30 s axios timeouts but no "You are offline" banner; mutations silently fail. POS-style flows in particular need an offline indicator + queued-write awareness. Fix: top-level `OfflineBanner` component listening to `online`/`offline` events that pauses React Query mutations or surfaces a persistent banner; `axios` interceptor that distinguishes "ECONNABORTED while offline" from real server errors.
  <!-- meta: scope=web/components/layout; files=packages/web/src/components/layout/AppShell.tsx; fix=add-OfflineBanner-listening-to-online-offline-events+react-query-online-manager-or-network-mode-config -->

- [ ] WEB-FO-005. **[HIGH] CommunicationPage SMS reminders write `localStorage[sms_reminders]` via read-modify-write with no synchronization — two tabs setting reminders concurrently lose one of them.** `pages/communications/CommunicationPage.tsx:1093-1099`. `JSON.parse(getItem) → push → setItem` race: tab A reads `[r1]`, tab B reads `[r1]`, A writes `[r1, r2]`, B writes `[r1, r3]` → r2 vanishes. Also no quota check (a reminder loop could blow the 5 MB budget). Same RMW pattern at `pages/tickets/TicketDetailPage.tsx:362-369` for `recent_views`. - [ ] WEB-FO-006. **[MED] Header notification poll re-issues HTTP every 30 s in addition to WS NOTIFICATION_NEW invalidation — duplicate work, doubles backend load on the bell counter.** `components/layout/Header.tsx:97-123`. The WS map already maps `NOTIFICATION_NEW → ['notification-count']`, so unread count auto-invalidates on every new notification. The 30 s setInterval adds redundant `notificationApi.unreadCount()` + `smsApi.unreadCount()` calls. With 50 active web sessions per tenant that's 100 wasted requests/min. Fix: drop the 30 s poll; rely on WS for invalidation. Keep only the visibility-resume fetch as a recovery for missed WS events while tab was hidden.

- [ ] WEB-FO-007. **[MED] DashboardPage runs ~13 independent useQuery calls each with their own `refetchInterval` (60 s, 120 s) — no shared scheduler, no jitter, all fire near-synchronously after mount.** `pages/dashboard/DashboardPage.tsx:449,461,861,869,877,1185,1510,1632,1649,1655,1661,1668,1676,1685`. After 60 s, ~7 queries refetch in the same tick → server sees a thundering-herd burst from every dashboard tab on every minute boundary. Multiply by tenant count + tabs and dashboard becomes the noisiest endpoint. - [ ] WEB-FO-009. **[MED] Header.tsx `fetchUnreadCount` / `fetchSmsUnreadCount` use raw axios (not React Query) and have no AbortController — request issued on tab-switch fires even after Header unmounts (logout race) and `setSmsUnreadCount` fires on an unmounted component.** `components/layout/Header.tsx:80-123`. - [ ] WEB-FO-012. **[MED] Optimistic-update mutations use `JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(old))` to deep-clone the React Query cache — drops `Date` objects, undefined values, and is O(n) on every drag/keystroke for large lists.** `pages/tickets/TicketDetailPage.tsx:259,322`, `KanbanBoard.tsx:155`, `TicketListPage.tsx:896,959,1014`, `TicketSidebar.tsx:426`, `TicketNotes.tsx:74`, `CommunicationPage.tsx:1109,1130`. On the kanban board with 200 tickets, a single drag triggers a full deep-clone (~5-10 ms hot, 50 ms+ on a slow tablet). Fix: use `structuredClone()` (broadly available since 2022) which preserves Dates/Maps; or use Immer's `produce` for surgical updates. Cheaper: shallow-clone only the slice being mutated.

- [ ] WEB-FO-013. **[MED] No navigation guard on in-flight mutations — clicking a sidebar link mid-mutation lets the request keep firing into a destroyed page; rollback `onError` toasts then surface on an unrelated route.** `pages/tickets/TicketDetailPage.tsx`, `KanbanBoard.tsx`, `TicketSidebar.tsx`. ### Wave-Loop Finder-M run 2026-04-24 — dead-code + duplicates + cleanup

- [x] WEB-FM-001. - [x] WEB-FM-002. ### Wave-Loop Finder-W run 2026-04-24 — vite config + heavy imports + lazy routes

- [x] WEB-FW-001. FIXED-by-Fixer-Y 2026-04-25 — added `build.rollupOptions.output.manualChunks` splitting vendor-react (react/react-dom/react-router-dom), vendor-charts (recharts), vendor-query (@tanstack/react-query), vendor-icons (lucide-react). **[HIGH] `vite.config.ts` `build` block has zero chunk strategy — no `rollupOptions.output.manualChunks`, so the 68 lazy routes share a single vendor chunk (recharts ~500kB + react + tanstack + lucide all bundled together for the dashboard).** `vite.config.ts:58-61` declares only `outDir` + `sourcemap:false`. With recharts imported by 4 pages (`InvoiceListPage:5`, `ReportsPage:17`, `reports/components/CustomerAcquisitionTab:5`, `reports/components/TechnicianHoursTab:5`) and 195 lucide-react imports across the app, every initial page load drags the full chart library even when not on `/reports` or `/invoices`. Vite's default heuristic puts all `node_modules` into one big `vendor.js` — first-paint regression for tenant subdomains.
  <!-- meta: scope=web/vite; files=packages/web/vite.config.ts:58-61,packages/web/src/pages/invoices/InvoiceListPage.tsx:5,packages/web/src/pages/reports/ReportsPage.tsx:17; fix=add-build.rollupOptions.output.manualChunks={recharts:[recharts,d3-*],vendor-react:[react,react-dom,react-router-dom],vendor-data:[@tanstack/react-query,@tanstack/react-table],vendor-icons:[lucide-react]}+enable-build.target=es2022 -->

Combined with WEB-FM-019 (no CI lint/typecheck scripts) the build never fails on bundle-size regression. ### Wave-Loop Finder-AC run 2026-04-25 — animations + reduced-motion

- [x] WEB-FAC-001. FIXED-by-Fixer-AA. **[HIGH] No global `prefers-reduced-motion` media query in `globals.css` — site-wide animations (~906 `animate-`/`transition-` usages, 632 `transition-*`) ignore vestibular accessibility setting.** `styles/globals.css:1-240` contains zero `@media (prefers-reduced-motion: reduce)` blocks; only 4 component-level checks exist (`useMilestoneToasts.ts:57`, `GettingStartedWidget.tsx:165`, `SuccessCelebration.tsx:76,80`) — all in onboarding. Toaster, Skeleton pulse, Loader2 spin, theme color transition (`html { transition: background-color 0.2s }`) all run regardless of OS setting. WCAG 2.3.3 (AAA) + 2.2.2 (A) violation for users with motion sensitivity. Add `@media (prefers-reduced-motion: reduce) { *, *::before, *::after { animation-duration: 0.01ms !important; transition-duration: 0.01ms !important; } }`.
  <!-- meta: scope=web/styles; files=packages/web/src/styles/globals.css:1-240; fix=add-@media-prefers-reduced-motion-reduce-block-zero-out-animation+transition-globally+keep-essential-state-changes -->

- [ ] WEB-FAD-001. **[HIGH] DashboardPage.tsx fires 11 separate `refetchInterval` queries (60s/120s) that all run regardless of tab visibility — when the dashboard is mounted, every minute the user's network sees an 11-request burst even with the tab in the background.** `DashboardPage.tsx:449,461,861,869,877,1185,1510,1632,1649,1655,1661,1668,1676,1685` — TanStack Query polls each independently while default `refetchOnWindowFocus` (set false in `main.tsx:100`) doesn't gate `refetchInterval`. There's also no `refetchIntervalInBackground: false` (defaults to false in v4+, but per-query polls still drift). Replace overlapping endpoints with a single aggregate `/dashboard/summary` query, OR add `refetchIntervalInBackground: false` + bump intervals to 120s minimum. WS already invalidates `['dashboard']` on TICKET_STATUS_CHANGED + PAYMENT_RECEIVED — polling is double-coverage.
