If server adds an `'owner'` or `'kiosk'` role, every callsite drifts silently. Import `ROLE_PERMISSIONS` from `@bizarre-crm/shared` and derive role gates from a single map.
  <!-- meta: scope=web/components+pages; files=packages/web/src/components/layout/Header.tsx:439,packages/web/src/components/layout/Sidebar.tsx:147,packages/web/src/pages/settings/SettingsPage.tsx:1761-1762,packages/web/src/pages/dashboard/DashboardPage.tsx:1626; fix=import-ROLE_PERMISSIONS-from-shared+derive-isAdminOrManager-from-canonical-map+add-eslint-rule-no-hardcoded-role-string-literal -->

- [ ] WEB-FAE-007. **[MED] `Sidebar.tsx:333` `useQuery({ queryKey: ['my-queue', user?.id] })` IS user-scoped, but neighboring `MyQueuePage` (`team/MyQueuePage.tsx:58`) and `TicketHandoffModal.tsx:61` use `['my-queue']` / `['team', 'my-queue']` without `user?.id` — three different shapes for one logical query.** Sidebar widget cache and page cache desync, and after `switchUser()` the page may briefly render the previous user's queue. `TicketHandoffModal`'s invalidate on assign-out doesn't touch the sidebar widget cache (different key shape), so handoffs leave stale rows in the widget until manual refetch. Standardize on `['my-queue', userId]` everywhere; combine with WEB-FAE-004 tenant prefix → `[tenantId, 'my-queue', userId]`.
  <!-- meta: scope=web/components+pages; files=packages/web/src/components/layout/Sidebar.tsx:333,packages/web/src/pages/team/MyQueuePage.tsx:58,packages/web/src/components/team/TicketHandoffModal.tsx:61; fix=standardize-queryKey-['my-queue',userId]+invalidate-with-same-shape -->

- [ ] WEB-FAE-008. **[MED] `DashboardPage.tsx:1684` `useQuery({ ..., enabled: role === 'manager' })` fetches manager-only team metrics, but if the user logs out and a new admin (not manager) logs in same tab, React Query keeps the previous manager's data cached under the same key and may briefly show it during the moment between `auth-cleared` and the new render.** `enabled` only stops fetching, doesn't clear cache. Cache-clear listener at `main.tsx:110` covers this IF event fires; cross-tab path (FAE-004 race) doesn't. Server returns 403 for non-managers but the cached "stale" data still satisfies `useQuery` until `gcTime` expires (default 5min). Fix by adding `role` to the queryKey: `['team-metrics', role]` so manager/admin/tech each have isolated caches.
  <!-- meta: scope=web/pages/dashboard; files=packages/web/src/pages/dashboard/DashboardPage.tsx:1684; fix=add-role-to-queryKey:['team-metrics',role]+OR-gcTime:0-on-role-gated-queries -->

- [ ] WEB-FAE-009. **[MED] `authStore.ts:168` cross-tab `storage` listener does NOT validate that the new identity belongs to the SAME tenant as the prior session — silently re-hydrates from `/auth/me` regardless.** If tab 2 in a different tenant clobbers `accessToken` (corrupt extension, kiosk shared device, leftover token from past session), tab 1's storage handler calls `checkAuth()` → `/auth/me` returns the new tenant's user → tab 1 silently swaps tenant context with no warning. Add a tenant-id mismatch guard: capture `oldUser.tenant_id` before `checkAuth`, compare with response, and on mismatch hard-redirect to `/login` with "Account changed in another tab" toast instead of swapping in place.
  <!-- meta: scope=web/stores; files=packages/web/src/stores/authStore.ts:149-175; fix=add-tenant_id-mismatch-guard-in-storage-handler+hard-redirect-on-cross-tenant-clobber -->

- [ ] WEB-FAE-010. **[LOW] `useDraft.ts:46-51` iterates ALL `localStorage` keys to GC old drafts but matches by name pattern only — has no tenant/user filter, so a user who logs out leaves draft text (potentially PII / customer notes / SMS body) in localStorage indefinitely until matching keys are GC'd by age.** Drafts may include customer addresses, ticket descriptions, internal SMS body. `auth-cleared` listener should also wipe `draft:*` keys synchronously on logout. Currently best-effort age-based GC at `useDraft.ts:51` only fires when the next user happens to mount a draft-using component — meaning the next user can read prior drafts via DevTools.
  <!-- meta: scope=web/hooks; files=packages/web/src/hooks/useDraft.ts:44-55; fix=on-auth-cleared-iterate-localStorage-and-removeItem-for-keys-matching-/^draft:/ -->
